PS C:\Windows\System32> function Get-WmiHelpLocation {  
param ($WmiClassName=’Win32_BIOS’)
  $Connected = [Activator]::CreateInstance([Type]::GetTypeFromCLSID([Guid]’{DCB00C01-570F-4A9B-8D69199FDBA5723B}’)).IsConnectedToInternet 
   if ($Connected)  
    {      $uri = ‘http://www.bing.com/search?q={0}+site:msdn.microsoft.com’ -f $WmiClassName
      $url = (Invoke-WebRequest -Uri $uri -UseBasicParsing).Links |      Where-Object href -like ‘http://msdn.microsoft.com*’ |      Select-Object -ExpandProperty href -First 1      
      Start-Process $url  
      $url   } 
       else  {      Write-Warning ‘No Internet Connection Available.’  } 
       }
